### [307] [Unsupervised Skill Discovery for Agentic Data Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06416)
*Zhisong Qiu,Kangqi Song,Shengwei Tang,Shuofei Qiao,Lei Liang,Huajun Chen,Shumin Deng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出DataCOPE，一种无监督的验证器引导的技能发现框架，用于数据智能体。它通过从探索轨迹中提取验证信号，在报告式和分析式两种任务上分别使用自适应检查表验证器和答案一致性验证器，无需标注即可发现可复用的数据技能，在两个基准上平均提升9.71%和32.30%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据智能体需要可复用的程序性知识来增强推理能力，但传统方法依赖昂贵的标注监督，且不同分析格式的成功标准各异。因此，如何在无标注条件下自动发现高质量、可复用的数据分析技能成为核心问题。

Method: DataCOPE包含三个迭代协作模块：Data-Analytic Agent生成探索轨迹，Unsupervised Verifier从轨迹中提取验证信号，Skill Manager通过对比学习提取技能。针对报告式分析，使用自适应检查表验证器动态生成任务标准并评分；针对推理式分析，使用答案一致性验证器基于轨迹间的答案一致性和自一致性作为信号。

Result: 在Deep Data Research（报告式）和DABStep（推理式）两个基准上，DataCOPE在所有baseline上均取得一致提升。平均而言，报告式任务提升9.71%，推理式任务提升32.30%。

Conclusion: DataCOPE证明了无监督验证器引导的技能发现框架的有效性，能够在无需人工标注的情况下自动从探索轨迹中提取可复用技能，显著提升数据智能体的性能，并在两种不同的分析格式上均展现出良好的泛化能力。

Abstract: Inference-time skill augmentation provides a lightweight way to improve data-analytic agents by injecting reusable procedural knowledge without updating model parameters. However, discovering effective skills for data analysis remains challenging, as reliable supervision is expensive and success criteria vary across analytical formats. This raises the key question of how to discover reusable data-analysis skills from unlabeled exploration alone. We propose DataCOPE, an unsupervised verifier-guided skill discovery framework for data-analytic agents. DataCOPE derives verifier signals from the exploration trajectories and uses them to characterize relative quality or aggreement among trajectories. It iteratively coordinates a Data-Analytic Agent for trajectory generation, an Unsupervised Verifier for signal extraction, and a Skill Manager for contrastive skill distillation. For report-style analysis, we instantiate the verifier as an Adaptive Checklist Verifier that derives task-specific criteria, scores reports by verifiable coverage, and iteratively refines the checklist. For reasoning-style analysis, we instantiate it as an Answer Agreement Verifier that groups trajectories by answer agreement and uses self-consistency as an auxiliary signal. We evaluate DataCOPE on report-style analysis from Deep Data Research and reasoning-style analysis from DABStep. Across both settings, DataCOPE consistently improves held-out performance over baselines. Averaged across four model settings, DataCOPE improves the mean score by 9.71% and 32.30% on report-style and reasoning-style tasks respectively.

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly deployed on long-horizon tasks requiring sustained reasoning over extended interaction histories. Yet, their system-level behavior remains uncharacterized. We present the first systems characterization of agent memory. First, we introduce a system-oriented taxonomy classifying agent memory systems along four axes. Second, we build a phase-aware profiling harness attributing cost to construction, retrieval, and generation. Third, we characterize ten representative systems across two benchmark suites, uncovering how design choices shift cost across the write and read paths. Finally, we derive 10 system recommendations covering construction scheduling, capability floors, amortization via query volume, freshness-latency tradeoffs, and fleet-scale management.

Method: Vortex结合了Python嵌入式前端语言和以页面为中心的张量抽象，用于表达广泛的稀疏注意力算法，并配备了与现代LLM服务栈紧密集成的高效后端。

As a result, Vortex substantially accelerates the design and iteration of sparse attention algorithms. First, AI agents use Vortex to automatically generate and refine diverse algorithms, the best reaching up to $3.46\times$ higher throughput than full attention while preserving accuracy. ### [311] [Goedel-Architect: Streamlining Formal Theorem Proving with Blueprint Generation and Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06468)
*Jui-Hui Chung,Ziyang Cai,Zihao Li,Qishuo Yin,Rohit Agarwal,Simon Park,Rodrigo Porto,Narutatsu Ri,Ziran Yang,Shange Tang,Xingyu Dang,Hongzhou Lin,Mengdi Wang,Danqi Chen,Chi Jin,Liam H Fowl,Sanjeev Arora*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Goedel-Architect 是一个基于蓝图生成与精炼的智能体框架，用于 Lean 4 形式化定理证明。它首先生成形式化定义和引理的依赖图（蓝图），然后使用 Lean 证明器并行证明每个开放的引理节点，失败节点会驱动全局蓝图的精炼。在 MiniF2F-test 上达到 99.2% pass@1，PutnamBench 上达到 75.6% pass@1，结合自然语言提示后性能进一步提升，且成本比同类管道低 500 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有形式化定理证明方法主要采用递归引理分解策略，容易陷入无效策略的死循环，效率低下。作者希望提出一种更高效的蓝图驱动方案，避免无效递归，提升证明成功率并降低成本。

Method: Goedel-Architect 包含两个核心阶段：(1) 蓝图生成阶段——根据自然语言证明（可选）生成形式化定义和引理的依赖图；(2) 精益求精阶段——使用工具增强的 Lean 证明器并行证明开放引理节点，失败的节点反馈驱动全局蓝图的精炼和重构，形成闭环优化。

Result: 使用 DeepSeek-V4-Flash 作为基座模型，在 MiniF2F-test 上达到 99.2% pass@1，PutnamBench 上达到 75.6% pass@1。加入自然语言证明引导后：MiniF2F-test 达到 100%，PutnamBench 提升至 88.8%（597/672），IMO 2025 解决 4/6，Putnam 2025 解决 11/12，USAMO 2026 解决 3/6。成本比同类开源管道低 500 倍。

Conclusion: Goedel-Architect 通过蓝图生成+并行证明+失败驱动的精炼循环，显著提升了形式化定理证明的性能和效率，实现了开源管道最先进的水平，且成本极具优势。蓝图驱动的策略对比递归分解策略更具鲁棒性和可扩展性。

Abstract: We introduce Goedel-Architect, an agentic framework for formal theorem proving in Lean 4 centered on blueprint generation and refinement. A blueprint is a dependency graph of definitions and lemmas that builds up to the main theorem. First, Goedel-Architect generates a blueprint of formally stated definitions and lemmas, along with declared dependencies. This blueprint is optionally guided by a natural language proof. Then, a tool-equipped Lean prover component closes each open lemma node in parallel using relevant dependencies. Failed lemmas in turn drive refinement of the global blueprint. This strategy contrasts with other mainstream approaches which use recursive lemma decomposition, and can inefficiently loop on dead-end strategies. Using the open-weight DeepSeek-V4-Flash (284B-A13B) as the backbone, Goedel-Architect attains 99.2% pass@1 on MiniF2F-test and 75.6% pass@1 on PutnamBench. With an optional natural-language proof seeding the initial blueprint on the harder problems, we additionally close the remaining two MiniF2F-test problems (reaching 100%), lift PutnamBench to 88.8% (597/672), and solve 4/6 on IMO 2025, 11/12 on Putnam 2025, and 3/6 on USAMO 2026. This represents state-of-the-art performance for an open-source pipeline at a price point up to 500x less than comparable open-source pipelines.

</details>


### [312] [MLEvolve: A Self-Evolving Framework for Automated Machine Learning Algorithm Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06473)
*Shangheng Du,Xiangchao Yan,Jinxin Shi,Zongsheng Cao,Shiyang Feng,Zichen Liang,Boyuan Sun,Tianshuo Peng,Yifan Zhou,Xin Li,Jie Zhou,Liang He,Bo Zhang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MLEvolve 提出了一种基于LLM的多智能体自进化框架，通过Progressive MCGS树搜索、Retrospective Memory记忆机制和分层控制，在MLE-Bench上取得SOTA性能，并展现出跨领域泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLE智能体存在跨分支信息隔离、无记忆搜索和缺乏分层控制的问题，限制了长期优化能力，亟需一种能持续自我进化的多智能体框架。

Method: (1) Progressive MCGS：图结构树搜索，通过参考边实现跨分支信息流动，熵启发式渐进调度从广泛探索转向集中利用；(2) Retrospective Memory：冷启动领域知识库 + 动态全局记忆，支持经验检索与复用；(3) 解耦策略规划与代码生成，引入自适应编码模式实现稳定长周期迭代。

Result: 在MLE-Bench上，12小时预算（标准时间一半）下平均奖牌率和有效提交率均达到SOTA；在数学算法优化任务上超越AlphaEvolve等专用方法，展现强跨领域泛化能力。

Conclusion: MLEvolve通过图搜索、记忆机制和分层控制有效解决了长期自我进化中的关键瓶颈，为端到端机器学习算法发现提供了新的高性能范式。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly applied to long-horizon tasks such as scientific discovery and machine learning engineering (MLE), where sustained self-evolution becomes a key capability. However, existing MLE agents suffer from inter-branch information isolation, memoryless search, and lack of hierarchical control, which together hinder long-horizon optimization. We present MLEvolve, an LLM-based self-evolving multi-agent framework for end-to-end machine learning algorithm discovery. By extending tree search to Progressive MCGS, MLEvolve enables cross-branch information flow through graph-based reference edges and gradually shifts the search from broad exploration to focused exploitation with an entropy-inspired progressive schedule. To allow the agent to evolve with accumulated experience, we introduce Retrospective Memory, which combines a cold-start domain knowledge base with a dynamic global memory for task-specific experience retrieval and reuse. For stable long-horizon iteration, we further decouple strategic planning from code generation with adaptive coding modes. Evaluation on MLE-Bench shows that MLEvolve achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple dimensions including average medal rate and valid submission rate under a 12-hour budget (half the standard runtime). Moreover, MLEvolve also outperforms specialized algorithm discovery methods including AlphaEvolve on mathematical algorithm optimization tasks, demonstrating strong cross-domain generalization. Our code is available at https://github.com/InternScience/MLEvolve.

</details>

### [313] [Availability-Aware and Efficiency-Driven AI Service Chain Provisioning in Multi-Domain Edge Intelligence Cloud](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05637)
*Hanzhi Chang,Jing Bai,Xin Tang,Xiaomei Liu,Yiming Chen*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于图与时间的多智能体AI服务链部署方法（GT-MAAISCP），用于解决多域边缘智能云中AI服务链的协作优化问题，在部署成本、延迟和可用性方面优于基准方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多域边缘智能云由多个网络运营商管理，AI服务以虚拟网络功能链（AISC）的形式交付。由于环境异构性、资源约束和信息可见性有限，以及AISC的时间依赖性，实现高效经济的AISC部署面临诸多挑战。

Method: 将AISC部署问题建模为部分可观测随机博弈（POSG），并提出GT-MAAISCP方法。每个智能体采用图-时间对偶网络（GTDN）架构，同时提取网络拓扑信息和时序关系，实现多智能体协作优化。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提方法在MDEIC中优于基准方法，并在不同网络拓扑和不同本地边缘云数量下展现了良好性能。

Conclusion: GT-MAAISCP有效解决了多域边缘智能云中AI服务链的部署问题，在成本、时延和可用性三者之间实现了协同优化。

Abstract: In a multi-domain edge intelligence cloud (MDEIC) managed by multiple network operators, AI services are delivered by chains of virtual network functions (VNFs) executed in sequence, called AI service chains (AISCs). Therefore, achieving an efficient and economical AISC provisioning approach is essential. However, the interaction between the environmental characteristics (heterogeneity, resource constraints and limited information visibility) of MDEIC and the time-dependence of AISCs, introduces various challenges to AISC provisioning in MDEIC. In this paper, we first formulate the AISC provisioning problem as a partially observable stochastic game (POSG). Then, we propose a graph-and-time-based multi-agent AISC provisioning (GT-MAAISCP) approach to achieve the collaborative optimization of AISC provisioning cost, delay and availability. Specifically, each agent uses the graph-time dueling network (GTDN) architecture to extract network topology information and temporal relationships. Finally, the experimental results demonstrate that the proposed approach outperforms benchmark approaches in MDEIC and also illustrate its performance under varying network topologies and different numbers of local EICs (LEICs).

### [314] [AISC deployment in dynamic UAV-assisted MEC network: a reinforcement learning method based on heterogeneous graph attention neural network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05722)
*Hanzhi Chang,Jing Bai,Xin Tang,Xiaomei Liu*

Completing an AI service requires multiple inferences, each of which is implemented by an AI service chain consisting of multiple virtual network functions (VNFs). The application of AISC relies on an efficient AISC deployment strategy to determine which UAV to deploy VNF on. However, the UMEC network topology is highly dynamic due to the high-speed movement of UAVs or their departure/arrival, which makes the AISC deployment in the UMEC network challenging. In addition, the intricate relationships between UMEC environment and AISC, as well as between individual VNFs in an AISC, can also affect the effectiveness of AISC deployment strategy. Moreover, under the constraints of energy consumption and load balancing, it is also difficult to optimize the AISC strategy to minimize AISC completion time for enhancing the quality of AI service. To address the above challenges, this paper proposes a double deep attention Q-network based on heterogeneous graph neural networks, which incorporates heterogeneous graph to capture diverse relationships in UMEC and utilizes attention mechanisms to adaptively focus on critical nodes and links for intelligent AISC deployment. The experimental results demonstrate that the proposed algorithm performs excellently in AISC completion time, AISC completion rate, load balancing and energy consumption.

This paper investigates energy-saving opportunities based on these strategies in a real 5G NSA deployment, utilizing a dataset provided by a European Mobile Network Operator. Using Key Performance Indicators from the dataset, we propose a data-driven framework to evaluate the energy-saving and QoS tradeoff when selectively deactivating underutilized 5G cells and offloading their traffic to 4G cells with enough resources within the same sector and site. Our results demonstrate network-wide cell switch-off opportunities ranging from 17% to 79%, while ensuring data rates between 25 Mbps and 5 Mbps, respectively.

This paper presents a machine learning (ML)-based energy saving strategy, trained using a real-world dataset from a European mobile operator, that enforces operator-defined policies that jointly consider strong throughput requirements and maximum outage tolerance constraints. ### [318] [DAST: A VLM-LLM Framework for Cross-Interface Anomaly Detection in O-RAN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06261)
*Francesco Spinelli,Esteban Municio,Pau Baguer,Gines Garcia-Aviles,Xavier Costa-Perez*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: DAST是一种零样本多智能体框架，通过VLM→LLM→VLM三级流水线，将O-RAN多变量KPI转换为视觉表征并利用领域知识进行跨接口异常检测，在真实测试集上达到0.910 F1-Score，优于传统时序异常检测方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统时序异常检测方法在面对O-RAN中标签稀缺、威胁演化快、高维多变量遥测数据时失效，需要一种无需重新训练即可跨接口检测DoS和性能降级攻击的新方法。

Method: 提出DAST框架，采用零样本多智能体架构，包含三个阶段：首先VLM将多变量KPI流转换为可视化表征；然后LLM对每个接口的文本描述进行O-RAN领域知识评分；最后VLM在高分辨率热图上验证可疑结果，输出问题接口、异常时间区间、O-RAN WG11对齐的影响评级及决策理由。

Result: 在真实O-RAN测试平台的网络轨迹上评估，在代表性性能降级场景下达到0.910 F1-Score和0.843 Accuracy，超越现有最先进的时序异常检测基线。

Conclusion: DAST通过视觉-语言多智能体协作，有效解决了O-RAN开放架构下跨接口异常检测的零样本泛化难题。

Abstract: O-RAN enables a disaggregated baseband stack with programmable functions that communicate over standardized open interfaces. The same openness that enables multi-vendor composition also expands the attack surface across logically decoupled tiers that make up the compute continuum. Among these threats, Denial-of-Service and performance-degradation attacks, which account for the majority of catalogued O-RAN threats, are particularly difficult to detect. Traditional Time-Series Anomaly Detection (TSAD) methods fail in this new regime where labelled baselines are scarce, threats evolve faster than detectors can be retrained, and the high-dimensional multivariate telemetry overwhelms monolithic inference models. To address these challenges, we present DAST, a zero-shot multi-agent framework for cross-interface anomaly detection in O-RAN that chains a three-stage VLM $\rightarrow$ LLM $\rightarrow$ VLM pipeline. DAST converts multivariate KPI streams into visual representations, scores textual per-interface descriptions against O-RAN domain knowledge, and verifies suspects on high-resolution heatmaps to output the problematic interfaces, the anomalous time intervals, an indicative O-RAN WG11-aligned operational impact rating and the decision rationale. We evaluate DAST on real network traces collected from an O-RAN testbed under representative performance degradation scenarios, achieving 0.910 F1-Score and 0.843 Accuracy, outperforming state-of-the-art TSAD baselines.

### [320] [Annotation of Positive vs Negative User Interactions for Social Sign Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06425)
*Biancamaria Bombino,Chiara Boldrini,Andrea Passarella,Marco Conti*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出利用大语言模型（LLM）在零样本设定下识别交互中的个人表扬与攻击，作为推断社交关系正负符号的更直接指标，解决了传统情感分析将话题情感与关系性质混为一谈的问题。实验表明LLM在此任务上表现良好，其中攻击检测鲁棒性更强，表扬检测则对模型和提示设计更敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有社交关系符号推断方法依赖情感分析标注单次交互的正负性再聚合，但情感分析捕捉的是内容的情感色彩而非交互本身的关系性质，这种混淆会导致系统性误分类。因此需要更直接的交互级关系信号识别方法。

Method: 提出利用LLM在零样本设定下识别交互中的个人表扬（positive）和个人攻击（negative）作为社交关系的直接指示符；使用四种模型（Qwen2.5:7b, Gemma2:9b, GPT-4o, GPT-5.4-mini）和三种复杂度递增的提示设计，在两个人工标注数据集（约298和340条文本）上进行评估。

Result: 零样本LLM在两项任务上均取得良好分类性能，无需任务特定训练数据即可建立关系标注的实用基线；攻击检测对提示设计和模型选择鲁棒，而表扬检测对两者均更敏感，反映了正面关系姿态具有更大的主观性。

Conclusion: 该研究为将基于LLM的关系标注整合到社交关系符号预测流程中奠定了基础。

Abstract: Inferring the sign of social relationships from online interactions is a fundamental challenge in social network analysis. Existing approaches typically rely on sentiment analysis to label individual interactions as positive or negative, then aggregate these labels to assign a sign to the relationship. However, sentiment analysis captures the valence of the content being discussed rather than the nature of the relational exchange itself, a conflation that can lead to systematic misclassification. In this paper, we propose a methodology that addresses this limitation by leveraging Large Language Models (LLMs) in a zero-shot setting to identify interaction-level relational signals (specifically, personal praise and personal attacks directed at the interlocutor) as more direct indicators of positive and negative social ties. We evaluate four models spanning open-weight and proprietary architectures (Qwen2.5:7b, Gemma2:9b, GPT-4o, GPT-5.4-mini) across three prompt designs of increasing complexity, on two human-annotated datasets of approximately 298 and 340 texts respectively. Results show that zero-shot LLMs achieve good classification performance on both tasks without any task-specific training data, establishing a practical baseline for relational annotation. Performance differs across tasks: attack detection is robust to prompt design and model choice, while praise detection is more sensitive to both, reflecting the greater subjectivity of positive relational gestures. These findings lay the groundwork for integrating LLM-based relational annotation into sign prediction pipelines.

</details>

### [321] [DeployBench: Benchmarking LLM Agents for Research Artifact Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05238)
*Yuanli Wang,Yaoyao Qian,Yue Zhang,Hanhan Zhou,Jindan Huang,Tianfu Fu,Qiuyang Mang,Huanzhi Mao,Wenhao Chai,Wendong Fan,Liqiang Jing*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出 DeployBench，一个包含 51 个跨领域（AI/ML、计算机系统、科学计算）研究工件部署任务的基准测试，评估了四种 SOTA LLM 代理（OpenHands），发现通过率仅为 7.8%-51.0%，主要失败原因（63%）是代理过早自我终止，未能满足论文特定的验证目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有环境部署基准无法覆盖研究工件部署的全范围挑战（多语言工具链、GPU/CUDA 等系统级依赖、遗留工件兼容性），而 LLM 代理往往假设已有可运行环境，实际部署从零搭建仍是一大瓶颈。

Method: 构建 DeployBench——51 个来自 AI/ML、计算机系统、科学计算领域的研究工件部署任务，每个任务有隐藏验证流水线执行论文指定实验并检查输出。使用 OpenHands 框架评估四种 SOTA LLM。

Result: 四种 LLM 的通过率仅 7.8%-51.0%。154 次失败中 97 次（63%）是代理自我终止，代理的完成前检查验证了比论文要求更弱或不同的目标。

Conclusion: DeployBench 揭示了当前 LLM 代理与自主部署之间的巨大差距，为科学研究的代理系统提供了现实测试平台。

Abstract: LLM agents have made rapid progress on software engineering and ML research tasks, but these advances often assume access to a working runnable environment. For research artifacts released alongside published papers, setting up such an environment from a fresh machine remains a major bottleneck. Existing environment setup benchmarks do not cover the full scope of research artifact deployment, which involves multi-language toolchains, system-level dependencies beyond containers (e.g. GPU/CUDA and kernel configurations), and legacy artifact compatibility. We introduce DeployBench, a multi-domain benchmark of 51 research-artifact deployment tasks spanning AI/ML, computer systems, and scientific computing, covering all these dimensions. Each task is verified by a hidden pipeline that executes the paper's designated experiment and checks its outputs. Evaluating four state-of-the-art LLMs with OpenHands yields pass-rates from 7.8% - 51.0% . Failures are dominated by a completion-judgment problem: 97 of 154 are agent-terminated self-stops, where the agent's pre-finish checks validate a different or weaker target than the paper-specific task requires. DeployBench highlights the gap between current agents and autonomous deployment, and offers a realistic testbed for scientific research agents.

</details>


### [322] [SWE-InfraBench: Evaluating Language Models on Cloud Infrastructure Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05249)
*Natalia Tarasova,Enrique Balp-Straffon,Aleksei Iancheruk,Yevhenii Sielskyi,Nikita Kozodoi,Liam H. Byrne,Jack Butler,Dayuan Jiang,Marcin Czelej,Andrew Ang,Yash Shah,Roi Blanco,Sergei Ivanov*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了SWE-InfraBench，一个针对基础设施即代码（IaC）的评估基准，聚焦于AWS CDK的增量代码编辑任务。评估显示，即使最先进的LLM（Sonnet 3.7）也仅能达到34%的成功率，表明当前模型在IaC开发方面存在显著局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM在软件工程领域取得了显著进展，但其在基础设施即代码（IaC）开发方面的能力尚未被充分探索。现有IaC基准主要集中于声明式范式（如Terraform）且涉及从头生成完整代码，缺乏对实际企业开发中常见的增量代码编辑任务的评估。

Method: 构建了SWE-InfraBench数据集，该数据集来源于数十个真实世界的IaC代码库，使用AWS CDK（命令式工具）。每个任务要求模型基于自然语言指令对现有代码库进行修改，并通过提供的测试用例判定是否成功。任务涉及对云资源依赖关系和实现模式的复杂推理。

Result: 最佳模型Sonnet 3.7仅成功34%的案例，专门推理模型DeepSeek R1仅达24%成功率，表明当前LLM在处理IaC代码编辑任务方面存在显著局限。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在IaC开发任务上表现不佳，亟需进一步提升模型对云资源依赖关系和增量代码修改的理解能力。

Abstract: Building infrastructure-as-code (IaC) in cloud computing is a critical task, underpinning the reliability, scalability, and security of modern software systems. Despite the remarkable progress of large language models (LLMs) in software engineering -- demonstrated across many dedicated benchmarks -- their capabilities in developing IaC remain underexplored. Unlike existing IaC benchmarks that predominantly center on declarative paradigms such as Terraform and involve generating entire codebases from scratch, our benchmark reflects the incremental code edits common in enterprise development with imperative tools like the AWS CDK. We present SWE-InfraBench, a diverse evaluation dataset sourced from dozens of real-world IaC codebases that challenge LLMs to perform realistic code modifications in AWS CDK repositories. Each example requires models to implement changes to existing codebases based on natural language instructions, with success determined by passing provided test cases. These tasks demand sophisticated reasoning about cloud resource dependencies and implementation patterns beyond conventional code generation challenges. Our evaluation results reveal significant limitations in current LLMs showing that even state-of-the-art systems struggle with many tasks -- the best model, Sonnet 3.7, succeeds in only 34\% of cases, while specialized reasoning models like DeepSeek R1 achieve just 24% success. The SWE-InfraBench dataset is available at: https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/64e59070fd51c0278560b01eb5dc4f3c447d5268cdabe5a350d2969e4413fea5

### [323] [A Taxonomy of Runtime Faults in Model Context Protocol Servers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05339)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCP协议在增强LLM的工具交互能力方面被广泛采用，但引入了新的可靠性挑战（如配置参数被接受但不被执行），而此前缺乏对这类运行时故障特征的实证研究。

Method: 采用自下而上的开放编码程序，手动分析了来自473个活跃MCP服务器GitHub仓库的837个运行时故障线程，构建分类体系；并通过55名MCP服务器开发者问卷调查评估外部效度。

Result: 分类体系包含11个顶级类别和27个子类别（73种叶子故障类型），涵盖协议交互、工具调用、模式执行、状态管理、模型-提供者集成、安全验证、超时和取消操作等维度。调查中开发者平均报告经历过20/27个子类别，没有类别未被观察到。

Abstract: MCP (Model Context Protocol) enables LLMs (Large Language Models) to interact with external tools and data sources via a standardized protocol. Its rapid adoption in tool-augmented Artificial Intelligence (AI) workflows has introduced new reliability challenges, such as configuration parameters that are accepted but not enforced at runtime, leading to unintended default behavior, whose runtime fault characteristics remain empirically unexamined. We present the first empirical taxonomy of runtime faults in MCP servers. We manually analyzed 837 MCP-specific runtime fault threads from 473 actively maintained MCP server GitHub repositories and derived a taxonomy using a bottom-up open coding procedure. The taxonomy comprises 11 top-level categories and 27 subcategories (73 leaf fault types), covering recurrent failures across protocol interactions, tool invocations, schema enforcement, state management, model-provider integration, security validation, and timeouts or explicit cancellations of in-progress operations. To assess the taxonomy's external validity, we surveyed 55 MCP server developers. Respondents reported experiencing an average of 20 of the 27 fault subcategories, and no category remained unobserved. These results indicate that the taxonomy reflects widely observed runtime failures in MCP-based systems and shall assist AI software maintenance and evolution in the future.

Existing research on agent oversight is largely conceptual; normative frameworks exist, but how users actually oversee agents is less known. In this paper, we bridge this gap by providing early empirical anchors for the theoretical discourse on agent oversight. Drawing on interviews with 17 experienced developers, we conduct an exploratory inquiry examining what forms of emergent oversight work developers perform, when, and how. We also document the oversight challenges developers face and the strategies they have started using to address them. We found at least four forms of emergent oversight work: a priori control, co-planning, real-time monitoring, and post hoc review. We show that oversight work is not only reactive and retrospective, as portrayed in existing research, but also preventative and proactive. We describe situated oversight challenges (e.g., difficulty reviewing agent-generated code) and outline heuristics developers adopt to address such challenges (e.g., using test results as guarantees for code correctness). We conclude with high-level takeaways, future research directions, implications for the human-centered design of software agents and for software engineering practice, and limitations of our research.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 识别出23个语义连贯的RE主题，归为6大高层类别；RE讨论以实用和任务导向为主，强调调试、反编译和系统级分析；内存、固件和文件格式分析相关主题呈现高难度和高未解决率。

  In this paper, we present REStack, a large-scale dataset of RE discussions collected from Stack Overflow and the dedicated Reverse Engineering Stack Exchange site. The dataset comprises over 12,000 RE-related posts spanning more than 15 years. Using Latent Dirichlet Allocation (LDA) with Genetic Algorithm (GA)-based hyperparameter optimization, followed by manual topic labeling, we identify 23 semantically coherent RE topics grouped into six high-level thematic categories. The dataset is further enriched with metadata and difficulty indicators derived from community interaction signals, such as unanswered rates and response times.
  Our analysis reveals that RE discussions are predominantly practical and task-oriented, with strong emphasis on debugging, decompilation, and system-level analysis, while topics related to memory, firmware, and file format analysis exhibit high difficulty and unresolved rates. Beyond empirical characterization, REStack provides a reusable resource for empirical studies, educational research, and the development and evaluation of AI- and LLM-based developer assistance tools for RE. By releasing the dataset and accompanying scripts, this work aims to facilitate reproducible research and advance data-driven support for RE practice.

### [326] [ADK Arena: Evaluating Agent Development Kits via LLM-as-a-Developer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05548)
*Jintao Huang,Xiaomin Li,Gaurav Mittal,Yu Hu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出LLM-as-a-Developer方法，构建ADK Arena自动化管道，系统评估51个Python ADK框架在四个基准上的表现。发现成功率57%，成本差异5.6倍，无单一框架主导，最佳框架解决80%任务但中位数仅32%，文档、源码和参数知识可互相替代。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Agent开发框架（ADK）数量激增，但缺乏对不同框架如何影响智能体性能的实证理解，需要一种系统化、可重复的方法来比较框架。

Method: 提出LLM-as-a-Developer方法，用LLM编码智能体替代人类开发者，学习框架API后编写并迭代修复代码。实现ADK Arena自动化管道，包含Docker隔离、三级验证流程和四个基准适配器（SWE-bench、τ²-bench、Terminal-Bench、MCP-Atlas），评估51个Python ADK框架。

Result: (1) 生成成功率57%，成本差异5.6倍（$0.6-$3.4），但成本与成功率无关；(2) 无单一框架主导，最佳框架解决80%任务（超越前沿编码智能体），中位数仅32%；(3) 框架使用率在28-40%之间，文档、源码和参数知识可互相替代。

Conclusion: 框架选择对智能体性能有显著影响但无绝对胜者，成本和API复杂度不作为成功预测指标；文档等外部资源并非硬瓶颈，不同信息来源可互相替代，为框架选择和开发提供实证指导。

Abstract: The rapid proliferation of Agent Development Kits (ADKs), SDK-level frameworks for building LLM-powered autonomous agents, has outpaced any empirical understanding of how framework choice affects agent performance. We propose \textbf{LLM-as-a-Developer}, a methodology that replaces human developers with an LLM coding agent that learns each framework's API from documentation, writes agent code, and iteratively repairs it through a validate-and-feedback loop until tests pass. By holding the developer constant and varying only the framework, generation effort becomes a quantitative proxy for API usability and the resulting agents provide a controlled measure of framework effectiveness. We implement this in \textbf{ADK Arena}, a fully automated pipeline with per-framework Docker isolation, a three-level validation pipeline, and benchmark adapters for SWE-bench, $τ^2$-bench, Terminal-Bench, and MCP-Atlas. Evaluating all 51 popular Python ADK frameworks (204 agent--benchmark pairs), we find that: (1)~generation succeeds for 57\% of runs, and its cost varies 5.6$\times$ across frameworks (\$0.6 to \$3.4 per agent), a quantitative proxy for API complexity, though cost alone does not predict success; (2)~no single framework dominates: the best single-benchmark ADK agents resolve up to 80\% of tasks and can even \emph{beat} general-purpose frontier coding agents at a fraction of the cost, yet the median framework resolves only 32\%; (3)~across information-source ablations, genuine framework usage stays within a narrow 28--40\% band (highest with raw source access and still 33\% with no reference material at all), indicating that documentation, source code, and parametric knowledge are largely substitutable rather than any one being a hard bottleneck.

In this paper, we propose SmellBench, an extensible code refactoring benchmark that proactively injects code smells into clean code snippets from real-world repositories. This design enables the generation of controlled, high-quality, and diverse refactoring cases with human-written ground truth. Specifically, it contains 294 cases spanning 7 popular smell types, 3 difficulty levels, 2 instruction settings across 7 real-world repositories. We further design 3 evaluation aspects covering functional correctness, localization ability, and refactoring quality assessment. Experiments with 2 popular agents and 6 large langauge models (LLMs) show that the best combination - Qwen Code + Claude Sonnet 4.5 - achieved only a 50.34 score of smell elimination. Main category: cs.SE

Abstract: For over half a century, software engineering has operated on a foundational premise: human engineers decompose problems, encode decision logic into static code, and manually adapt that code as requirements evolve. This paper argues that the emergence of AI agents -- systems where large language models serve as the primary reasoning engine, dynamically generating and discarding code as an instrumental resource -- constitutes not an incremental improvement but a fundamental restructuring of the software paradigm. Drawing on first-principles analysis of complexity scaling, we formalize the distinction between traditional software (where code is the carrier of decision logic) and agentic systems (where code is ephemeral tooling for an LLM-driven reasoning loop). We trace the historical arc from licensed software to SaaS to what we term Agent-as-a-Service (AaaS), showing that each shift transferred additional complexity away from end-users. We introduce the concept of Agentic Engineering as an emergent discipline -- distinct from software engineering in its core object of study, control model, and human role. Through analysis of recent benchmark evidence including SWE-bench Verified, EvoClaw, and LangChain's multi-agent coordination studies, we demonstrate both the transformative potential of the agentic paradigm and its current limitations. We conclude with a four-stage roadmap toward self-evolving agent ecosystems and concrete recommendations for practitioners navigating this transition.

### [329] [Enhancing Software Engineering Through Closed-Loop Memory Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05646)
*Xuehang Guo,Zora Zhiruo Wang,Qingyun Wang,Graham Neubig,Xingyao Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出MemOp，一个面向软件工程智能体的闭环记忆增强框架，通过将记忆效用建立在经过验证的下游影响上，既作为任务无关的评估基准，也作为无需标注的优化信号。实验表明，该方法在单次和跨次记忆增强中均能提升智能体性能，成功率和解决效率分别提升最高5.25%和4.63%，同时计算成本降低至少9.79%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM驱动的SE智能体存在根本性局限：每次任务都从零构建上下文并重复类似错误，缺乏跨任务的经验积累、提炼和复用能力。即使有记忆机制，也缺少一个原则性的、任务无关的记忆效用度量，导致难以严格评估或跨智能体跨场景泛化。

Method: 提出MemOp闭环框架，将记忆效用锚定在"经过验证的下游影响"上，使其同时具备两个功能：1) 任务无关的评估基准（可衡量记忆质量），2) 无需人工标注的优化信号（可自动指导记忆策略改进）。框架同时支持单次记忆增强（同任务内）和跨次记忆增强（跨任务复用）。

Result: 实验结果表明：成功率绝对提升最高5.25%，解决效率绝对提升最高4.63%，计算成本降低至少9.79%。

Conclusion: MemOp通过将记忆效用与下游任务验证结果绑定，提供了一种原则性的记忆增强方案，有效打破了SE智能体"零经验累积"的局限，并在多个维度上取得了显著改进。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have enabled powerful software engineering (SE) agents capable of navigating complex codebases and resolving real-world issues. However, these agents remain fundamentally episodic: they fail to retain, refine, and reuse experiences across tasks, repeatedly reconstructing context from scratch and reproducing similar mistakes. Even with memory support, they offer no remedy for the absence of a principled, task-agnostic \textit{memory utility}, making them difficult to evaluate rigorously or generalize across agents and settings. To tackle these limitations, we introduce \ours, a closed-loop framework for memory augmentation in SE agents. \ours grounds memory utility in \textit{validated downstream impact}, establishing utility as both a task-agnostic \textbf{evaluation benchmark} and an annotation-free \textbf{optimization signal}. Through complementary evaluation on \textit{single-episode} and \textit{cross-episode} memory augmentation, results demonstrate that \ours consistently improves SE agents across settings, achieving absolute gains of up to $\uparrow5.25\%$ in success rate and $\uparrow4.63\%$ in resolve efficiency, while substantially reducing computational cost by $\geq9.79\%$. Our project page: \href{https://xhguo7.github.io/MemOp/}{https://xhguo7.github.io/MemOp/}.

### [330] [Where Do Large Language Models Fail on Competitive Programming? A Taxonomy of Failures by Algorithm Type and Difficulty Rating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05228)
*Ayush Kumar Jha,Shalini Jha*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 系统研究了LLM在Codeforces编程竞赛中的失败模式，发现Chain-of-Thought推理会严重损害GPT-4o性能（46.0%→36.8%），并使Claude的编译错误飙升244%，且错误答案（WA）是主要的未通过判决类型。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: CoT使GPT-4o通过率从46.0%降至36.8%（Greedy逻辑缺陷加剧）；Claude在CoT下通过率63.5%但编译错误增加244%（从9到31）；WA占GPT-4o未通过解的90%以上，占Claude的约70%。

Conclusion: 标准提示工程技术（如CoT）无法弥合LLM在竞赛编程环境中的算法推理鸿沟，反可能引入新的性能退化。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate increasing proficiency on competitive programming benchmarks, yet technical reports predominantly publish aggregate pass rates, obscuring domain-specific vulnerabilities. We present a systematic empirical study of LLM failure patterns using a balanced taxonomy of 315 Codeforces problems across seven algorithm categories and three difficulty tiers. We evaluate GPT-4o and Claude Sonnet 4.6 under strict execution-based conditions, controlling for temperature (T = 0.2). To isolate the impact of reasoning frameworks on algorithmic correctness, we conduct an ablation study comparing direct zero-shot generation against zero-shot Chain-of-Thought (CoT). Our findings reveal a severe divergence from standard NLP benchmarks: forcing CoT aggressively penalizes GPT-4o, dropping its pass rate from 46.0% to 36.8% and exacerbating a critical weakness in Greedy logic. Conversely, while Claude maintains a higher logical baseline (63.5% under CoT), the expanded text generation severely degrades its markdown instruction adherence, causing its Compile Errors to more than triple (from 9 to 31, a 244% increase). Furthermore, failure-mode analysis indicates that Wrong Answer (WA) is the dominant verdict for both models--accounting for over 90% of GPT-4o's and roughly 70% of Claude's unaccepted solutions. These findings empirically demonstrate that standard prompt engineering techniques fail to bridge the algorithmic reasoning gap in competitive programming environments.

</details>


### [331] [When Surface Form Changes Moderation Decisions: A Paired Study of Code-Mixed Workflow Instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05654)
*Suraj Babu Thimma Krishnaram*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究在多语言混合输入（泰米尔语-英语混合）下，仇恨言论审核系统的工作流程变化，发现相比纯英语输入，混合语言输入会导致更高的决策翻转率（26.5%），增加审核负担和误报率，而简单的不一致延迟规则虽能减少错误但会增加审核工作量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用配对评估设计：相同内容分别以纯英语和泰米尔语-英语混合形式表达；阈值基于纯英语开发数据调优；对比两种输入下的决策稳定性（翻转率）、审核负担（review rate）和误报率（non-hate false-flag rate）；额外比较纯泰米尔语输入以区分语言覆盖局限与混合语言不稳定性；测试基于不一致性的延迟规则。

Conclusion: 工作流级别的评估能揭示传统分类指标无法捕捉的审核失败模式；代码混合输入会显著降低审核系统的稳定性和效率；当前系统存在语言覆盖局限，而非仅限于混合语言不稳定性问题。

Abstract: Hate moderation is often evaluated as classification on clean English inputs, but deployed systems must route content to actions such as ALLOW, FLAG, or REVIEW. We study how this workflow changes under code-mixed inputs using a paired evaluation setting where the same underlying content is expressed as clean English and Tamil-English code-mix. Under thresholds tuned on clean English development data, code-mixed inputs produce substantial action instability, with a paired clean- to-code-mix decision flip rate of 0.265. The main workflow effects are increased review burden and increased false-flagging of non-hateful content: review rate rises from 0.138 to 0.297 and non-hate false-flag rate rises from 0.069 to 0.104. Tamil-only inputs show stronger degradation overall, suggesting a broader language-coverage limitation rather than the same code-mixed instability pattern. A simple disagreement-based deferral rule reduces automatic errors on stressed inputs, but only by increasing review load. These results show that workflow-level evaluation reveals moderation failures that standard classification summaries can miss.

*Mohammad Zare,Omid Abdolrahmani*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型和AI编码代理在软件开发中面临上下文窗口管理的结构性挑战：注入完整项目文档和代码会导致中间信息丢失、token成本飙升和架构漂移。亟需一种更高效、更精确的上下文管理方法。

Method: 模仿微服务思想，将知识封装为原子化、范围精确的"技能胶囊"（skill capsules），由动态路由器根据任务语义相关性选择并激活最匹配的胶囊，将上下文分配建模为受token预算约束的语义相关性优化问题。

Conclusion: MicroSkill Architecture为构建AI原生开发系统提供了可扩展的基础，能实现更高效、更可靠且具备进化能力的开发环境。

Abstract: Large language models and AI coding agents have reshaped software development, but the path to fully AI-native systems faces structural challenges. Chief among them is managing context windows without losing accuracy or efficiency. When developers inject full project documentation and code into a model's memory, the model loses mid-sequence information, token costs spiral, and architecture drifts. This paper presents MicroSkill Architecture: a modular design paradigm inspired by microservices, applied to knowledge encapsulation instead of service decomposition. Instead of feeding an agent the entire codebase, the architecture partitions knowledge into atomic, sharply scoped skill capsules, and a dynamic router selects only semantically relevant capsules for the task. We formally model context allocation as constrained optimization over semantic relevance subject to a token budget. An empirical case study an enterprise content management system with fifteen complex features shows that MicroSkill cuts token consumption by over 90%, nearly doubles first-try compilation success rates, eliminates architectural violations entirely, and enables autonomous extraction and registration of seven new skill capsules via a self-learning mechanism. These findings suggest MicroSkill Architecture offers a scalable foundation for building AI-native development systems that are more efficient, more reliable, and capable of evolving over time.

At the same time, the flood of AI suggestions, prompts, and possible solutions can leave developers mentally stretched. ### [334] [Towards Persistent Case-Based Memory for Autonomous Data Science: A CBR-Augmented R&D-Agent with a Locally Deployable Small Language Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05250)

TL;DR: 本文提出CBR-augmented R&D-Agent，将基于案例推理（CBR）的持久化层集成到微软R&D-Agent框架中，并首次评估Gemma 4 31B Dense作为自主数据科学智能体主干的可行性。在两个Kaggle竞赛上，CBR方法在Spaceship Titanic任务上准确率略高于基线（0.8147 vs 0.8098），且方差显著降低。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将CBR持久化层集成到微软R&D-Agent框架中，使用Gemma 4 31B Dense作为后端。CBR层通过单个环境变量切换，覆盖三个R&D循环阶段。案例以结构化记录存储，包含可执行代码快照和质量元数据。采用五门质量过滤器和启发式重用检测机制（结合嵌入相似度、代码指纹重叠和注入溯源）评估知识迁移效果。

Result: 在两个Kaggle竞赛（NOMAD 2018、Spaceship Titanic）上，使用四种随机种子各执行8个改进循环。CBR方法在Spaceship Titanic上准确率优于基线（0.8147 vs 0.8098，d=-1.41），方差显著降低。108次检索事件中，平均嵌入相似度0.882（高语义相关性），平均代码指纹相似度0.305（低结构相似性），表明是概念性指导而非逐字复制。

Conclusion: CBR增强方法能有效提升小型自主数据科学智能体的性能稳定性和知识迁移能力，Gemma 4作为本地可部署SLM主干具有可行潜力，且CBR提供的是概念性指导而非代码抄袭，具有实用价值。

Abstract: Most top-performing autonomous data-science agents rely on frontier cloud models and lack persistent, cross-session memory. This paper addresses two open gaps: (1) the underexplored use of formally structured, quality-controlled Case-Based Reasoning (CBR) case bases coupling symbolic case records with executable code artefacts; and (2) the untested viability of Small Language Models (SLMs) as locally deployable agent backbones. We present CBR-augmented R&D-Agent, integrating a persistent CBR layer into Microsoft's R&D-Agent framework with a custom backend for Gemma 4 31B Dense -- the first published end-to-end evaluation of Gemma 4 as an autonomous data-science agent backbone. The CBR layer overrides three R&D loop phases via a surgical subclass toggled by a single environment variable. Cases are stored as structured records with executable code snapshots and quality metadata; a five-gate quality filter and a heuristic reuse-detection mechanism assess knowledge transfer by combining embedding similarity, code-fingerprint overlap, and injection provenance. Evaluated on two Kaggle competitions (NOMAD 2018, Spaceship Titanic) with four seeds over eight improvement loops each, CBR achieves directionally higher accuracy than the CBR-disabled baseline on Spaceship Titanic (0.8147 vs. 0.8098, d = -1.41) with substantially lower variance. Each task is resolved through a closed loop: a Code Agent generates a web project, a UI Agent executes test cases on the deployed site, and a User LLM turns evaluation outcomes into natural-language feedback for the next round. Abstract: Multiple machine learning models can achieve near-equivalent predictive performance on the same task, yet provide divergent feature-based explanations. This is called the Rashomon effect of (explainable) machine learning, and it raises the question of which explanations, if any, are trustworthy. ### [337] [TLA-Prover: Verifiable TLA+ Specification Synthesis via Preference-Optimized Low-Rank Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06133)
*Eric Spencer,Arslan Bisharat,Brian Ortiz,Khushboo Bhadauria,TaiNing Wang,George K. Thiruvathukal,Konstantin Laufer,Mohammed Abuhamad*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出TLA-Prover，一个200亿参数的大模型，用于TLA+形式化规约合成。通过监督微调+基于修复的GRPO强化学习（以TLC模型检查器直接作为奖励信号），模型在30个问题的基准上达到Gold和Diamond级别各30%的通过率（pass@1），是未调优基线（8.6%）的约3.5倍。Gold与Diamond指标在所有检查点保持一致，杜绝了平凡属性失效模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TLA+是验证分布式系统和安全关键协议的形式化规约语言，但大语言模型生成的TLA+规约经常因语义错误无法通过TLC模型检查器（25个LLM中最佳基线仅26.6%语法通过、8.6%语义通过），亟需提升模型生成TLA+规约的正确性。

Method: 采用两阶段训练：首先在已验证示例上进行监督微调（SFT），然后使用基于修复的组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行强化学习，模型学习修复自身被拒绝的规约。另外训练了直接偏好优化（DPO）变体作为消融。TLC模型检查器直接提供奖励信号，无需训练奖励模型。输出分四个等级：Bronze（语法通过）、Silver（无警告）、Gold（通过TLC）、Diamond（TLC检测到修改后规约的违例）。

Result: 在30个问题的保留基准上，TLA-Prover在Gold和Diamond级别均达到9/30（pass@1=30%），是未调优基线8.6%的约3.5倍。DPO变体在Diamond级别达到20%。Gold和Diamond在所有检查点始终一致，有效防止了平凡属性失效模式。

Conclusion: TLA-Prover通过结合SFT与基于TLC反馈的GRPO训练，显著提升了LLM生成正确TLA+规约的能力，且无需学习奖励模型。Gold与Diamond的一致性设计确保了模型不会生成语义平凡的伪正确规约。

Abstract: TLA+ is a formal specification language for verifying distributed systems and safety-critical protocols. Large language models (LLMs) frequently produce TLA+ specifications that fail the TLC model checker for semantic reasons. Across 25 LLMs, the best public baseline is 26.6% syntactic parse and 8.6% semantic model-check. We present TLA-Prover, a 20-billion-parameter model for TLA+ specification synthesis. Training combines supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on verified examples with repair-based group-relative policy optimization (GRPO). In the GRPO stage, the model learns to fix its own rejected specifications. We also train a direct preference optimization (DPO) variant from the same SFT checkpoint as an ablation. TLC provides the reward signal directly, with no learned reward model. Four tiers grade each output: Bronze (parses), Silver (no warnings), Gold (passes TLC), and Diamond. To reach Diamond, the model's correctness property is automatically altered in a small way; TLC must then detect a violation. If TLC still passes, the property was always-true and contributes nothing; the output fails Diamond. TLA-Prover reaches 9/30 (i.e. pass@1 = 30%) at both Gold and Diamond on a held-out 30-problem benchmark. This is roughly 3.5x the 8.6% untuned baseline. The DPO variant reaches 20% at Diamond. Gold and Diamond coincide at every checkpoint; this prevents the trivial-property failure mode.

*Isabella Graßl,Christopher Lazik,Shalini Chakraborty,Grischa Liebel,Miguel Goulão*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究通过问卷调查发现，在软件建模教育中，学生对与社会相关的领域（如社会公益问题）有更高的学习动机，并且希望拥有选择权；而教育者则高估了学生对学习相关领域的兴趣。研究揭示了教师假设与学生偏好之间的脱节，并指出微小的设计选择可能导致学生被排除在外。学生认为只有当反馈被明显采纳时才有意义。因此，建议采用以学生为中心的领域选择策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究集中于建模工具、符号和评估，但很少关注问题领域的选择以及其带来的多样性、相关性和文化视角如何塑造学生的学习体验。本研究旨在探索问题领域和教学方法如何影响建模教育中的动机、参与度、包容性和反馈。

Method: 对90名学生和22名教育者进行平行问卷调查，收集关于问题领域、教学方法对动机、参与度、包容性和反馈影响的定量与定性数据。

Result: 学生对与社会相关的领域表现出最强的动机，并偏好自主选择；教育者则高估了学生对与学习相关领域的兴趣。发现教师假设与学生偏好之间存在脱节，且微小的设计选择可能导致学生感到被排斥。学生认为只有当反馈被明显采纳时才有意义。

Conclusion: 包容性的领域选择是学生动机的核心，建议采用以学生为中心的领域选择策略。

Abstract: Student engagement is critical for effective learning in software modelling, yet fostering motivation and inclusivity remains a challenge. While existing research has focused on modelling tools, notations, and assessment, little attention has been given to how the choice of problem domains and the diversity, relatability, and cultural perspectives they bring shape students' learning experiences. This study explores how problem domains and teaching methods influence motivation, engagement, inclusiveness, and feedback in modelling education. To investigate these dimensions, we conducted parallel surveys with 90 students and 22 educators. Our findings reveal disconnects between educator assumptions and student preferences: Students show greatest motivation for socially relevant domains and prefer choice in selection, while educators overestimate interest in study-related domains. The study identifies how minor design choices can exclude students. Students perceive feedback as meaningful when visibly acted upon. These findings suggest inclusive domain selection is central to student motivation; thus, we recommend student-centred domain selection.

### [340] [More than a Judge: An Empirical Study of Agent-Human Interaction in Crowdsourced Testing Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06301)
*Yue Wang,Yuan Zhao,Shengcheng Yu,Zhenyu Chen,Qing Gu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过20名测试者在4阶段对照实验中发现，基于多智能体评估生成的反馈不仅能提高测试报告修订质量，还能帮助测试者在后续新任务中提交更好的初始报告，并展现出部分跨应用的能力迁移。问卷反馈也支持这一结论，但指出反馈在具体性和可执行性上仍有改进空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作已证明LLM多智能体评估与人类共识高度一致，但自动化评判本身不足以说明智能体输出能否嵌入工作流并真正改进人类工作。本文研究这一缺失问题，探究评估衍生的可操作反馈能否提升测试者的报告修订能力、后续任务表现以及跨应用实践迁移。

Method: 设计四阶段对照人类受试者实验：20名测试者在3个真实应用上完成报告任务。智能体基于文本性、充分性和竞争力三个维度生成反馈。通过比较修订报告质量、新任务首次提交表现以及跨应用迁移效果来评估反馈的有效性，并用17人问卷补充定性分析。

Result: 智能体生成的反馈能即时提升修订报告质量；在暴露反馈后，测试者在新任务上的首次提交表现更好；部分但有意义的能力迁移到后续应用。问卷显示反馈总体可理解、被用于修订并延续到后续任务，但在具体性和可执行性方面仍有摩擦。

Conclusion: 在众包测试场景下，评估智能体不仅能作为事后评判者，还能作为工作流集成的反馈提供者，支持上游报告质量改进。

Abstract: Agentic AI is increasingly being integrated into software engineering workflows. In crowdsourced testing, however, the large volume and uneven quality of submitted reports still create a substantial review burden for developers. In prior work, we developed and validated a multi-agent assessment backbone based on the LLM-as-a-Judge paradigm. That backbone assesses reports along three dimensions--textuality, adequacy, and competitiveness--and was shown to align well with human consensus while substantially reducing assessment effort. Yet reliable automated judging does not by itself show whether agent outputs can improve human work when embedded into workflow. This paper studies that missing question in the context of crowdsourced testing. We investigate whether assessment-derived, actionable feedback can improve how testers revise reports, perform on later tasks, and transfer reporting practices across applications. To do so, we conducted a controlled four-stage human-subject study with 20 testers across three real-world applications. The results show that agent-generated feedback supports immediate improvements in revised reports, better first submissions on a new task after prior feedback exposure, and evidence of partial but meaningful transfer to a later application. A post-task questionnaire completed by 17 participants complements these artifact-based findings by suggesting that the feedback was generally understandable, acted upon in revision, and carried into later tasks, while also revealing remaining friction in specificity and execution. Overall, the study provides empirical evidence that, in the studied crowdsourced testing setting, assessment agents can serve not only as post-hoc judges but also as workflow-integrated feedback providers that support upstream report-quality improvement.

</details>


### [341] [From Failed Trajectories to Reliable LLM Agents: Diagnosing and Repairing Harness Flaws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06324)
*Mengzhuo Chen,Junjie Wang,Zhe Liu,Yawen Wang,Qing Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出HarnessFix框架，通过追踪轨迹诊断智能体故障并自动修复编排层（ETCLOVG），在多个基准上提升15.2%-50.0%性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自改进方法无法精确定位失败轨迹中的责任证据及导致不可靠行为的编排层，修复范围过大或间接。

Method: 1) 将执行轨迹与编排代码编译为HTIR中间表示；2) 将故障归因到具体轨迹步骤和编排层；3) 将重复诊断聚合为可用缺陷记录，映射到修复算子；4) 生成并验证编排补丁。

Result: 在SWE-Bench Verified等四个基准上，修复后编排性能提升15.2%-50.0%，优于人工编排和自演化基线。

Conclusion: HarnessFix能有效诊断并修复智能体编排层缺陷，揭示跨ETCLOVG层的常见故障模式。

Abstract: LLM-based agents increasingly rely on harnesses that provide execution environments, tool interfaces, context, lifecycle orchestration, observability, verification, and governance. Existing self-improving agents and automatic harness evolution methods mainly improve agents through runtime supervision, prompt optimization, workflow search, or harness modification based on final outcomes. However, they often fail to diagnose where the responsible evidence lies in failed trajectories and which harness layer causes the unreliable behavior, resulting in broad, indirect, or poorly scoped changes. This paper proposes HarnessFix, a trace-guided framework for diagnosing agent failures and repairing agent harnesses. HarnessFix compiles raw execution traces and harness code into a Harness-aware Trace Intermediate Representation (HTIR), which normalizes fragmented trajectory evidence and captures step-level provenance and control-flow relations. It then attributes failures to responsible trajectory steps and harness layers, consolidates recurring diagnoses into actionable flaw records, and maps them to scoped repair operators. Finally, HarnessFix generates and validates harness patches under flaw-specific repair specifications to reduce target flaws without introducing unacceptable regressions. We evaluate HarnessFix on SWE-Bench Verified, Terminal-Bench 2.0 Verified, GAIA and AppWorld. Across these benchmarks, HarnessFix improves held-out test performance over the initial harnesses by 15.2%--50.0%, outperforms human-designed and self-evolution baselines, and reveals recurring harness-flaw patterns across ETCLOVG layers.

</details>


### [342] [Scaffold, Not Vocabulary? A Controlled, Two-Tier, Pre-Registered Study of a Popperian Code-Generation Skill](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06454)
*Mehmet Iscan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究发现，赋予大语言模型“波普尔式证伪主义”提示技能的效果主要来自指令的结构化框架，而非其波普尔式程序内容本身。在前沿模型上所有条件均触及性能天花板无法区分；在小模型上完整技能与仅保留标签的支架无显著差异，由此贡献了一个校准的负结果与可复用的消融协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实践表明，给LLM提供类似“波普尔证伪主义者”的提示技能能提升代码生成效果，但这些增益几乎全由LLM作为评判者（LLM-as-a-judge）测量，而该工具存在位置偏见、自我偏好和文体偏见。研究者质疑：增益究竟来自技能中的波普尔内容，还是来自任何支架都会施加的结构？

Method: 预注册的双层消融实验，包含三个对照组：长度匹配的安慰剂、仅保留波普尔式标题但剥离程序的标签支架、执行神谕（HumanEval+单元测试），以及词汇光环哨兵和同模型自我评判审计。在大模型（Claude Sonnet 4.6, N=163）和小模型（Qwen2.5-Coder-0.5B, N=164）上分别测试。

Result: 大模型上所有条件接近基准天花板，无法区分，预注册的+5点改进未被支持（天花板限制未检出）。小模型上结构化臂将best-of-eight正确率提升20-22点，但完整技能与仅标签支架无显著分离（F@8=L@8 vs V@8=34.8%），安慰剂仅落后2.4点。0.5B自我评判应用波普尔评分表无法超越随机选择，且将60%选择集中在单一索引上。

Conclusion: 在两种测试设定下，波普尔式程序内容未带来超出标签支架的可分离执行正确性收益，增益追踪的是支架结构。该研究贡献了校准的负结果和可复用的消融协议，结论限定了关于一类提示技能的工程主张，而非对波普尔方法论本身的评价。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly write, review, and judge code, and a fast-growing practice equips them with prompt 'skills' that ask the model to reason like a scientist. A prominent example tells the model to act as a Popperian falsificationist, and such skills are reported to improve generated code. But these gains are almost always read off an LLM-as-a-judge, an instrument with documented positional, self-preference, and stylistic biases. We ask: if it appears to help, is the gain from the skill's Popperian content, or from the structure any scaffold imposes? We pre-register a two-tier ablation with three controls: a length-matched placebo, a labels-only scaffold that keeps the Popperian headers but strips the procedure, and an execution oracle (HumanEval+ unit tests), plus a vocabulary-halo sentinel and a same-model self-judge audit. On a frontier model (Claude Sonnet 4.6, N=163) all conditions sit near the benchmark ceiling and do not separate, so the pre-registered +5-point improvement is not supported (a ceiling-limited non-detection). On a small model (Qwen2.5-Coder-0.5B, N=164) structured arms lift best-of-eight correctness by 20-22 points, but the full skill shows no separable benefit over a labels-only scaffold (aggregate F@8=L@8 vs V@8=34.8%), and the placebo trails by only 2.4 points. A 0.5B self-judge applying the Popperian rubric does not beat random selection and concentrates 60% of its picks on one index. In the two settings tested, the skill's Popperian procedural content adds no separable execution-correctness benefit beyond a labels-only scaffold, so the gains track scaffold structure. We contribute a calibrated negative result and a reusable disambiguation protocol; the finding bounds an engineering claim about one prompt-skill family and is not an evaluation of Popperian methodology in general.

</details>


### [343] [Code2LoRA: Hypernetwork-Generated Adapters for Code Language Models under Software Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06492)
*Liliana Hotsko,Yinxi Li,Yuntian Deng,Pengyu Nie*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出Code2LoRA，一个超网络框架，通过生成仓库特定的LoRA适配器来注入仓库级知识，无需推理时的token开销。支持静态仓库（Code2LoRA-Static）和演化仓库（Code2LoRA-Evo）两种场景。在自建基准RepoPeftBench上，静态任务匹配了per-repository LoRA上界，演化任务比单共享LoRA提升5.2个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码语言模型需要仓库级上下文来解决导入、API调用和项目约定问题。传统方法要么通过RAG或依赖分析注入长输入，要么对每个仓库进行微调或LoRA——这在仓库规模扩大时成本高昂且难以应对代码库演化。

Method: 提出Code2LoRA超网络框架，生成仓库特定的LoRA适配器。包含两个变体：Code2LoRA-Static（将单仓库快照转为适配器）和Code2LoRA-Evo（通过GRU隐藏状态按代码diff更新适配器）。同时构建RepoPeftBench基准，含604个Python仓库的静态和演化两个任务轨道。

Result: 静态任务：Code2LoRA-Static达到63.8%跨仓库和66.2%仓库内精确匹配，匹配per-repository LoRA上界。演化任务：Code2LoRA-Evo达到60.3%跨仓库精确匹配，比单共享LoRA高5.2个百分点。

Conclusion: Code2LoRA能有效地将仓库级知识注入代码语言模型，无需推理时额外token开销，且能适应代码库演化，是一种高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Code language models need repository-level context to resolve imports, APIs, and project conventions. Existing methods inject this knowledge as long inputs (retrieved through RAG or dependency analysis) or through per-repository fine-tuning and LoRA -- costly at repository scale and brittle to evolving codebases. We introduce Code2LoRA, a hypernetwork framework that generates repository-specific LoRA adapters, effectively injecting repository knowledge with zero inference-time token overhead. Code2LoRA supports two usage scenarios: Code2LoRA-Static converts a single repository snapshot into an adapter, suitable for comprehension of stable codebases; while Code2LoRA-Evo maintains an adapter backed by a GRU hidden state updated per code diff, suitable for active development of evolving codebases. To evaluate Code2LoRA against parameter-efficient fine-tuning baselines, we build RepoPeftBench, a benchmark of 604 Python repositories with two tracks: a static track with 40K training and 12K test assertion-completion tasks, and an evolution track with 215K commit-derived training and 87K commit-derived test tasks. On the static track, Code2LoRA-Static achieves 63.8% cross-repo and 66.2% in-repo exact match, matching the per-repository LoRA upper bound; on the evolution track, Code2LoRA-Evo achieves 60.3% cross-repo exact match (+5.2 pp over a single shared LoRA). Code2LoRA's code can be found at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/code2lora-6857; the model checkpoints and RepoPeftBench datasets can be found at https://huggingface.co/code2lora.

</details>


### [344] [STMutants: A Mutation Testing Dataset for Structured Text Programs in Industrial Automation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05499)
*Md Humaun Kabir,Md Rakibul Islam,Helen H. Lou*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文提出了STMutants，一个面向IEC 61131-3结构化文本（ST）程序的突变测试数据集，包含从11个工业ST程序中生成的108个有效突变体，覆盖7种突变算子类别。通过评估三个大语言模型（LLM）在测试用例生成和突变预测任务上的表现，验证了数据集的有效性，填补了PLC工业软件突变测试领域公开基准的空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ST程序广泛应用于可编程逻辑控制器（PLC）这一实时、安全关键的工业环境，软件故障可能导致设备损坏、生产损失或系统不安全行为。然而，目前ST程序领域缺乏支持可复现突变测试研究的公开基准数据集，这一缺口阻碍了相关自动化测试与质量保障研究的进展。

Method: 采用四阶段方法论构建突变体：(1) 故障类型分析与算子选择（覆盖值、关系、算术、逻辑、否定、操作插入/删除、初始化7类）；(2) 句法转换生成突变体；(3) 可编译性验证；(4) 人工等价突变筛选（评估者间一致性kappa=0.87）。数据集包含来自OSCAT基本库和工业来源的11个ST程序，生成110个一阶突变体，经可观测性与等价性筛选后保留108个。

Result: 三个大语言模型（LLM）在108个保留突变体上的突变检测准确率分别为86.1%、94.4%和86.1%，统计检验证实模型间存在显著性能差异。数据集覆盖7类突变算子，经严格等价与可观测性筛选，评估者间一致性高达0.87。

Conclusion: STMutants作为首个面向ST程序的公开突变测试基准数据集，支持自动化测试生成、突变分析、故障定位及AI辅助质量保障等方向的可复现研究，对提升PLC工业软件可靠性具有重要意义。

Abstract: Mutation testing is widely used to evaluate test-suite effectiveness, yet IEC 61131-3 Structured Text (ST) programs still lack a publicly available benchmark that supports reproducible mutation-based research. This gap is especially important because ST is extensively used in Programmable Logic Controllers (PLCs) that operate in real-time, safety-critical industrial environments, where software faults may cause equipment damage, production loss, or unsafe system behavior. To address this need, we present STMutants, a curated mutation testing dataset for industrial automation software. STMutants contains 110 generated first-order mutants derived from 11 ST programs collected from the OSCAT basic library and industrially relevant sources, of which 108 are retained after observability and equivalence screening. The dataset covers seven mutation operator categories adapted from classical taxonomies for the PLC domain, including value, relational, arithmetic, logical, negation, operation insertion/omission, and initialization faults. Each mutant is constructed through a four-phase methodology: fault-type profiling and operator selection, syntactic transformation, compilability verification, and manual equivalence screening with strong inter-rater agreement (kappa = 0.87). To demonstrate the usefulness of the dataset, we evaluate three large language models (LLMs) in a two-phase setting: test-suite generation followed by mutation kill/survive prediction. Across 108 retained mutants, the models achieve mutation detection accuracies of 86.1%, 94.4%, and 86.1%, respectively, with statistical analysis confirming significant performance differences. By providing the first publicly available mutation benchmark for ST programs, STMutants enables reproducible research on automated test generation, mutation analysis, fault localization, and AI-assisted quality assurance for PLC software.

</details>
